import java.net.URI;
import java.net.http.HttpClient;
import java.net.http.HttpRequest;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;

public class T {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        HttpClient client = HttpClient.newHttpClient();
        HttpRequest request = HttpRequest.newBuilder().uri(URI.create("http://foo.com/")).build();
        client.sendAsync(request, HttpResponse.BodyHandlers.ofString()).thenApply(HttpResponse::body).thenAccept(System.out::println).join();
    }
}

import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;

public class Temp {
  public static void main(String[] args) {
    String str = "2019-11-28";
    System.out.println("å­—ç¬¦æ˜¯å¦åŒ¹é…æ­£åˆ™ï¼š" + str.matches("^(\\d{4})-(\\d{1,2})-\\d{1,2}$"));
    // ^å¼€å§‹$ç»“æŸ
    Pattern p = Pattern.compile("^(\\d{4})-(\\d{1,2})-\\d{1,2}$", Pattern.CASE_INSENSITIVE);
    Matcher m = p.matcher(str);
    // findæŸ¥æ‰¾
    boolean find = m.find();
    if (!find) System.err.println("ä¸åŒ¹é…ï¼");;
    String group = m.group();
    System.out.println("æ˜¯å¦æ‰¾åˆ°åŒ¹é…ï¼š" + find + "\nå­—ç¬¦ä¸²ä¸­åŒ¹é…çš„å€¼ä¸ºï¼š" + group);
    // æ•è·ç»„ï¼Œæ¯ä¸€ä¸ªæ‹¬å·()éƒ½æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªæ•è·ç»„
    String group1 = m.group(1);
    String group2 = m.group(2);
    int groupCount = m.groupCount();
    System.out.println("æ•è·ç»„ä¸ªæ•°ï¼š"+groupCount);
    System.out.println("æ•è·ç»„ï¼š" + group1 + " - " + group2);
  }
}

Features

import org.apache.log4j.Logger;

/**
 * @author ChangSheng
 * @date 2020-03-19
 */
public class Log4jDemo {

    static Logger log = Logger.getLogger(Log4jDemo.class.getName());

    public static void main(String[] args) {
        log.trace("Trace Message!");
        log.debug("Debug Message!");
        log.info("Info Message!");
        log.warn("Warn Message!");
        log.error("Error Message!");
        log.fatal("Fatal Message!");
    }
}

public class SwaggerConfig {

    /** é…ç½®Swaggerï¼ˆé…ç½®docketä»¥é…ç½®Swaggerå…·ä½“å‚æ•°ï¼‰ï¼Œæ³¨è§£@Value("${swagger.enable}")ç”¨äºè·å–é…ç½®æ–‡ä»¶ä¸­çš„å€¼ */

    public Docket docket(@Value("${swagger.enable}") boolean swaggerEnable) {
        return new Docket(DocumentationType.SWAGGER_2)
                // è®¾ç½®æ˜¯å¦ä½¿ç”¨
                .enable(swaggerEnable)
                // é…ç½® API ä¿¡æ¯
                .apiInfo(new ApiInfo("é•¿ç”Ÿçš„ Api Documentation", "æˆ‘æè¿°ä¸€ä¸‹è¿™ä¸ªçš„ä½œç”¨: Api Documentation", "ç‰ˆæœ¬: 1.0",
                        "https://shengjava.com/", new Contact("é•¿ç”Ÿ", "https://shengjava.com/", ""),
                        "Apache 2.0", "http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0", new ArrayList<>()))
                // é…ç½®æ‰«ææ¥å£ï¼ˆselectæŒ‡å®šapisï¼Œé…ç½®RequestHandlerSelectorsï¼‰
                .select().apis(RequestHandlerSelectors.basePackage("com.sheng.swaggereg.controller")).build()
                .groupName("sheng");
    }
}
